    "trx": "Тип тормоза, используемый железнодорожными вагонами, который использует давление воздуха. Тормоза на автомобилях устроены таким образом, что они срабатывают при удалении воздуха из трубы.     "val": "Although a liver dialysis machine can be thought of as a sort of artificial liver, an actual liver carries out much more complicated metabolic reactions that dialysis cannot completely replace. For this reason, biohybrid liver replacements combining mechanical functions with active live liver cells from pigs are currently under research; with clinical tests have been conducted in the United States. The hope is that these bioartificial devices will some day be able to keep those with failed livers alive until the necessary transplants are available."
